const __universalAtob = function (b64Encoded) {
    try {
        let binary_string = atob(b64Encoded), len = binary_string.length, bytes = new Uint8Array(len);
        for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) {

        }
        return bytes;
    } catch (err) {
        return new Uint8Array(global.Buffer.from(b64Encoded, 'base64'));
    }
};
